The perceived \"lack of visual feedback\" is actually caused by a **different issue**: the binary copy fails with \"Text file busy\" error, but this error message gets lost in the TUI output.\n\n## Investigation Findings\n\n### 1. Keystroke Handling (Working Correctly)\n\n**Code path:**\n- `crates/forge-tui/src/event.rs:144-146` - Ctrl+U maps to `AppEvent::Update`\n- `crates/forge-tui/src/app.rs:715-717` - `AppEvent::Update` calls `trigger_update()`\n- `crates/forge-tui/src/app.rs:759-808` - `trigger_update()` runs cargo build and attempts copy\n\n**Evidence from tmux capture:**\n```\nFinished `release` profile [optimized] target(s) in 0.25s\ncp: cannot create regular file '/home/coder/.cargo/bin/forge': Text file busy\n```\n\n### 2. Tmux Configuration (Not Interfering)\n\nThe only Ctrl+U binding in tmux is for `copy-mode-vi` (halfpage-up), which only activates when in copy mode. Normal mode passes Ctrl+U through to the application.\n\n### 3. Terminal Line-Kill (Not an Issue)\n\nThe standard `\\C-u: unix-line-discard` binding is irrelevant because:\n- forge-tui uses crossterm with `enable_raw_mode()`\n- Raw mode disables line editing and passes all keystrokes directly to the application\n\n### 4. Root Cause: Binary Copy Fails\n\nThe update process:\n1. ✅ Status message set: \"Rebuilding forge...\"\n2. ✅ Cargo build runs and succeeds\n3. ❌ `cp target/release/forge ~/.cargo/bin/forge` fails with \"Text file busy\"\n4. ⚠️ Error message shown but may not be visible (TUI rendering issue)\n\n**\"Text file busy\"** occurs because Linux prevents overwriting an executable file while it's running.\n\n## Visual Feedback Issues\n\nThe actual problems with visual feedback are:\n\n1. **Error message visibility**: The `cp` error appears in the TUI but gets rendered in an awkward location (blends with UI elements)\n2. **No persistent indication**: After the error, the status reverts but there's no clear indication the update failed\n3. **Blocking operation**: `child.wait()` blocks the TUI, preventing immediate visual feedback during the build\n\n## Recommended Fixes for fg-3cm\n\n### Short-term (Visual Feedback)\n1. **Add a dedicated \"Update Status\" widget** or modal that shows:\n   - \"Building...\" during cargo build\n   - \"Installing...\" during copy\n   - Success or failure result with clear error messages\n\n2. **Non-blocking execution**: Run the update in a separate thread with status polling\n\n### Long-term (Binary Replacement)\n1. **Use rename/move instead of copy**:\n   - Build to a temp location\n   - Rename/move the binary (atomic operation)\n   - This may still fail but is more robust\n\n2. **Exit-and-restart pattern**:\n   - Exit forge gracefully\n   - Have a wrapper script that runs the update then restarts forge\n   - This is the most reliable approach for self-updating binaries\n\n3. **Update indicator**: Show \"Update ready - restart required\" instead of trying to overwrite in-place\n\n## Artifacts\n\n- Key event handler: `crates/forge-tui/src/event.rs:144-147`\n- Update trigger: `crates/forge-tui/src/app.rs:759-808`\n- Update script: `update-forge.sh`\n\n## Conclusion\n\n**The investigation reveals that Ctrl+U is working correctly.** The issue reported as \"lack of visual feedback\" is actually a combination of:\n1. The update process failing silently (binary overwrite blocked)\n2. Error messages not being clearly displayed in the TUI\n3. No dedicated UI component for update status\n\nThe fix in fg-3cm should focus on better status display and handling the \"Text file busy\" scenario gracefully.\n","numLines":91,"startLine":1,"totalLines":91}}}

UpToDate,\n59\t    /// Update available with download details\n60\t    Available {\n61\t        /// Current version\n62\t        current: String,\n63\t        /// Latest available version\n64\t        latest: String,\n65\t        /// URL to download the binary\n66\t        download_url: String,\n67\t        /// Size of the asset in bytes\n68\t        asset_size: u64,\n69\t    },\n70\t}\n71\t\n72\t/// Progress information for download operations.\n73\t#[derive(Debug, Clone)]\n74\tpub struct DownloadProgress {\n75\t    /// Bytes downloaded so far\n76\t    pub downloaded: u64,\n77\t    /// Total bytes to download\n78\t    pub total: u64,\n79\t    /// Percentage complete (0-100)\n80\t    pub percent: u8,\n81\t}\n82\t\n83\t/// Result of a self-update operation.\n84\t#[derive(Debug, Clone)]\n85\tpub enum UpdateResult {\n86\t    /// Update completed successfully\n87\t    Success {\n88\t        /// Previous version\n89\t        old_version: String,\n90\t        /// New version\n91\t        new_version: String,\n92\t    },\n93\t    /// Update failed with error message\n94\t    Failed(String),\n95\t    /// Already up to date\n96\t    AlreadyUpToDate,\n97\t}\n98\t\n99\t/// GitHub release asset information.\n100\t#[derive(Debug, Deserialize)]\n101\tstruct GitHubAsset {\n102\t    name: String,\n103\t    #[serde(rename = \"browser_download_url\")]\n104\t    download_url: String,\n105\t    size: u64,\n106\t    state: String,\n107\t}\n108\t\n109\t/// GitHub release information from API.\n110\t#[derive(Debug, Deserialize)]\n111\tstruct GitHubRelease {\n112\t    #[serde(rename = \"tag_name\")]\n113\t    tag_name: String,\n114\t    assets: Vec<GitHubAsset>,\n115\t}\n116\t\n117\t/// Check for available updates from GitHub releases.\n118\t///\n119\t/// # Arguments\n120\t///\n121\t/// * `current_version` - Current version string (e.g., \"0.1.9\")\n122\t///\n123\t/// # Returns\n124\t///\n125\t/// - `UpdateStatus::UpToDate` if already on latest version\n126\t/// - `UpdateStatus::Available` with download details if update available\n127\t/// - `ForgeError` on network or parsing errors\n128\tpub async fn check_for_update(current_version: &str) -> crate::Result<UpdateStatus> {\n129\t    info!(\"Checking for updates (current: {})\", current_version);\n130\t\n131\t    let client = reqwest::Client::builder()\n132\t        .timeout(Duration::from_secs(API_TIMEOUT_SECS))\n133\t        .user_agent(USER_AGENT)\n134\t        .build()\n135\t        .map_err(|e| ForgeError::UpdateCheck {\n136\t            message: format!(\"Failed to create HTTP client: {}\", e),\n137\t        })?;\n138\t\n139\t    let response = client\n140\t        .get(GITHUB_RELEASES_API)\n141\t        .send()\n142\t        .await\n143\t        .map_err(|e| ForgeError::UpdateCheck {\n144\t            message: format!(\"Failed to fetch releases: {}\", e),\n145\t        })?;\n146\t\n147\t    if !response.status().is_success() {\n148\t        return Err(ForgeError::UpdateCheck {\n149\t            message: format!(\"GitHub API returned status {}\", response.status()),\n150\t        });\n151\t    }\n152\t\n153\t    let release: GitHubRelease = response\n154\t        .json()\n155\t        .await\n156\t        .map_err(|e| ForgeError::UpdateCheck {\n157\t            message: format!(\"Failed to parse release response: {}\", e),\n158\t        })?;\n159\t\n160\t    // Parse version from tag (e.g., \"v0.1.9\" -> \"0.1.9\")\n161\t    let latest_version = release.tag_name.strip_prefix('v').unwrap_or(&release.tag_name);\n162\t\n163\t    info!(\"Latest version: {}\", latest_version);\n164\t\n165\t    // Compare versions using semver\n166\t    if !is_newer_version(current_version, latest_version)? {\n167\t        info!(\"Already running latest version\");\n168\t        return Ok(UpdateStatus::UpToDate);\n169\t    }\n170\t\n171\t    // Find the appropriate asset for this platform\n172\t    let asset_name = get_asset_name_for_platform();\n173\t    let asset = release\n174\t        .assets\n175\t        .iter()\n176\t        .find(|a| a.name == asset_name && a.state == \"uploaded\")\n177\t        .ok_or_else(|| ForgeError::UpdateAssetNotFound {\n178\t            platform: asset_name.to_string(),\n179\t        })?;\n180\t\n181\t    info!(\n182\t        \"Update available: {} -> {} ({} bytes)\",\n183\t        current_version, latest_version, asset.size\n184\t    );\n185\t\n186\t    Ok(UpdateStatus::Available {\n187\t        current: current_version.to_string(),\n188\t        latest: latest_version.to_string(),\n189\t        download_url: asset.download_url.clone(),\n190\t        asset_size: asset.size,\n191\t    })\n192\t}\n193\t\n194\t/// Perform the self-update: download and atomic swap.\n195\t///\n196\t/// # Arguments\n197\t///\n198\t/// * `download_url` - URL to download the binary from\n199\t/// * `expected_size` - Expected size of the download in bytes\n200\t/// * `progress_tx` - Optional channel to send progress updates\n201\t///\n202\t/// # Returns\n203\t///\n204\t/// - `UpdateResult::Success` on successful update\n205\t/// - `UpdateResult::Failed` with error message on failure\n206\tpub async fn perform_update(\n207\t    download_url: &str,\n208\t    expected_size: u64,\n209\t    progress_tx: Option<Sender<DownloadProgress>>,\n210\t) -> crate::Result<UpdateResult> {\n211\t    info!(\"Starting update download from {}\", download_url);\n212\t\n213\t    // Get current executable path\n214\t    let current_exe = env::current_exe().map_err(|e| ForgeError::UpdateInstall {\n215\t        message: format!(\"Failed to get current executable path: {}\", e),\n216\t    })?;\n217\t\n218\t    // Download to a staging file\n219\t    let staging_file = get_staging_path(&current_exe)?;\n220\t\n221\t    info!(\"Downloading to staging file: {:?}\", staging_file);\n222\t\n223\t    // Download the new binary\n224\t    download_file(download_url, &staging_file, expected_size, progress_tx).await?;\n225\t\n226\t    // Verify the downloaded file is a valid executable\n227\t    verify_binary(&staging_file)?;\n228\t\n229\t    info!(\"Update download complete! Binary staged at {:?}\", staging_file);\n230\t\n231\t    Ok(UpdateResult::Success {\n232\t        old_version: env!(\"CARGO_PKG_VERSION\").to_string(),\n233\t        new_version: \"latest\".to_string(), // We don't have this info here anymore\n234\t    })\n235\t}\n236\t\n237\t/// Restart the process using the newly downloaded binary.\n238\t///\n239\t/// This function performs the following steps:\n240\t/// 1. Gracefully shutdown current process (caller's responsibility)\n241\t/// 2. Exec the new binary from staging location\n242\t/// 3. New process will rename itself to the final location\n243\t///\n244\t/// This function DOES NOT RETURN on success - it replaces the current process.\n245\t/// On error, it returns a ForgeError.\n246\tpub fn restart_with_new_binary() -> crate::Result<()> {\n247\t    info!(\"Initiating restart with new binary\");\n248\t\n249\t    // Get current executable path\n250\t    let current_exe = env::current_exe().map_err(|e| ForgeError::UpdateInstall {\n251\t        message: format!(\"Failed to get current executable path: {}\", e),\n252\t    })?;\n253\t\n254\t    // Get staging path\n255\t    let staging_file = get_staging_path(&current_exe)?;\n256\t\n257\t    // Verify staging file exists\n258\t    if !staging_file.exists() {\n259\t        return Err(ForgeError::UpdateInstall {\n260\t            message: format!(\"Staging file not found at {:?}\", staging_file),\n261\t        });\n262\t    }\n263\t\n264\t    info!(\"Staging file found at {:?}\", staging_file);\n265\t\n266\t    // Verify the staging file is executable\n267\t    verify_binary(&staging_file)?;\n268\t\n269\t    // Get the final install path (e.g., ~/.cargo/bin/forge)\n270\t    let install_path = get_install_path(&current_exe)?;\n271\t\n272\t    info!(\n273\t        \"Will exec staging binary and install to {:?}\",\n274\t        install_path\n275\t    );\n276\t\n277\t    // Set env vars directly in the process before execv() — exec inherits\n278\t    // the current environment. We must set these here (not on a Command\n279\t    // object) because exec_binary() uses raw execv(), not std::process::Command.\n280\t    // SAFETY: This is safe here because we are about to exec() — no other\n281\t    // threads can observe the inconsistent env state. The exec syscall\n282\t    // replaces the entire process image.\n283\t    unsafe {\n284\t        env::set_var(\"FORGE_INSTALL_PATH\", &install_path);\n285\t        env::set_var(\"FORGE_STAGING_PATH\", &staging_file);\n286\t        env::set_var(\"FORGE_AUTO_RESTART\", \"1\");\n287\t    }\n288\t\n289\t    // Preserve current args\n290\t    let args: Vec<String> = env::args().skip(1).collect();\n291\t\n292\t    info!(\n293\t        \"Execing new binary: {:?} with args: {:?}\",\n294\t        staging_file, args\n295\t    );\n296\t\n297\t    // Replace current process with new binary using exec\n298\t    // On Unix, use exec syscall to replace the process\n299\t    exec_binary(&staging_file, &args)?;\n300\t\n301\t    // This line should never be reached if exec succeeds\n302\t    unreachable!(\"exec() returned, which should never happen\");\n303\t}\n304\t\n305\t/// Check if a staged update needs to be installed.\n306\t///\n307\t/// This handles two scenarios:\n308\t/// 1. Auto-restart: env vars FORGE_AUTO_RESTART, FORGE_INSTALL_PATH, FORGE_STAGING_PATH\n309\t///    are set by the old process before execv()\n310\t/// 2. Manual restart: a stale staging file exists from a previous update that was\n311\t///    downloaded but the user quit instead of auto-restarting\n312\t///\n313\t/// Returns the install path if an update was installed, None otherwise.\n314\tpub fn check_and_perform_self_install() -> crate::Result<Option<PathBuf>> {\n315\t    // Determine staging and install paths\n316\t    let (staging_path, install_path) = if env::var(\"FORGE_AUTO_RESTART\").is_ok() {\n317\t        // Auto-restart path: env vars from old process\n318\t        info!(\"Detected auto-restart environment - performing self-install\");\n319\t\n320\t        let install_path_str = env::var(\"FORGE_INSTALL_PATH\").map_err(|_| {\n321\t            ForgeError::UpdateInstall {\n322\t                message: \"FORGE_INSTALL_PATH not set\".to_string(),\n323\t            }\n324\t        })?;\n325\t        let staging_path_str = env::var(\"FORGE_STAGING_PATH\").map_err(|_| {\n326\t            ForgeError::UpdateInstall {\n327\t                message: \"FORGE_STAGING_PATH not set\".to_string(),\n328\t            }\n329\t        })?;\n330\t        (PathBuf::from(staging_path_str), PathBuf::from(install_path_str))\n331\t    } else if let Some(staged) = has_staged_update() {\n332\t        // Manual restart path: stale staging file detected\n333\t        info!(\"Detected staged update from previous session - installing\");\n334\t\n335\t        let current_exe = env::current_exe().map_err(|e| ForgeError::UpdateInstall {\n336\t            message: format!(\"Failed to get current executable path: {}\", e),\n337\t        })?;\n338\t        let install = get_install_path(&current_exe)?;\n339\t        (staged, install)\n340\t    } else {\n341\t        return Ok(None);\n342\t    };\n343\t\n344\t    // Verify staging file still exists and is valid\n345\t    if !staging_path.exists() {\n346\t        warn!(\"Staging file disappeared: {:?}\", staging_path);\n347\t        return Ok(None);\n348\t    }\n349\t\n350\t    if let Err(e) = verify_binary(&staging_path) {\n351\t        warn!(\"Staged binary failed verification, removing: {}\", e);\n352\t        let _ = fs::remove_file(&staging_path);\n353\t        return Ok(None);\n354\t    }\n355\t\n356\t    info!(\n357\t        \"Installing from {:?} to {:?}\",\n358\t        staging_path, install_path\n359\t    );\n360\t\n361\t    // Create backup of old binary\n362\t    let backup_path = install_path.with_extension(\"old\");\n363\t    if install_path.exists() {\n364\t        info!(\"Backing up old binary to {:?}\", backup_path);\n365\t        if backup_path.exists() {\n366\t            fs::remove_file(&backup_path).map_err(|e| ForgeError::UpdateInstall {\n367\t                message: format!(\"Failed to remove old backup: {}\", e),\n368\t            })?;\n369\t        }\n370\t        fs::rename(&install_path, &backup_path).map_err(|e| ForgeError::UpdateInstall {\n371\t            message: format!(\"Failed to backup old binary: {}\", e),\n372\t        })?;\n373\t    }\n374\t\n375\t    // Move staging binary to install location.\n376\t    // rename() works on Linux even for running binaries (atomic directory op).\n377\t    // If cross-filesystem, fall back to copy+delete.\n378\t    let move_result = fs::rename(&staging_path, &install_path);\n379\t    if let Err(e) = move_result {\n380\t        // Cross-filesystem fallback: copy then delete\n381\t        info!(\"rename() failed ({}), falling back to copy\", e);\n382\t        fs::copy(&staging_path, &install_path).map_err(|e2| {\n383\t            // Try to restore backup on failure\n384\t            if backup_path.exists() {\n385\t                let _ = fs::rename(&backup_path, &install_path);\n386\t            }\n387\t            ForgeError::UpdateInstall {\n388\t                message: format!(\"Failed to install new binary: {}\", e2),\n389\t            }\n390\t        })?;\n391\t        let _ = fs::remove_file(&staging_path);\n392\t    }\n393\t\n394\t    // Set executable permissions\n395\t    fs::set_permissions(&install_path, fs::Permissions::from_mode(0o755)).map_err(|e| {\n396\t        ForgeError::UpdateInstall {\n397\t            message: format!(\"Failed to set executable permissions: {}\", e),\n398\t        }\n399\t    })?;\n400\t\n401\t    // Clean up environment variables (no-op if not set)\n402\t    // SAFETY: These environment variables are only used during the update process\n403\t    // and are safe to remove as we're done with them.\n404\t    unsafe {\n405\t        env::remove_var(\"FORGE_AUTO_RESTART\");\n406\t        env::remove_var(\"FORGE_INSTALL_PATH\");\n407\t        env::remove_var(\"FORGE_STAGING_PATH\");\n408\t    }\n409\t\n410\t    // Save the new version to ~/.forge/version\n411\t    let current_version = env!(\"CARGO_PKG_VERSION\");\n412\t    if let Err(e) = save_current_version(current_version) {\n413\t        warn!(\"Failed to save version file: {}\", e);\n414\t    }\n415\t\n416\t    info!(\"Self-install complete! Running from {:?}\", install_path);\n417\t\n418\t    Ok(Some(install_path))\n419\t}\n420\t\n421\t/// Get the staging path for the downloaded binary.\n422\t///\n423\t/// Uses a stable path (not PID-dependent) so the staged update survives\n424\t/// manual restarts. The staging file is placed in a forge-specific temp dir.\n425\tfn get_staging_path(_current_exe: &Path) -> crate::Result<PathBuf> {\n426\t    let temp_dir = std::env::temp_dir().join(\"forge-update\");\n427\t    if !temp_dir.exists() {\n428\t        fs::create_dir_all(&temp_dir).map_err(|e| ForgeError::UpdateInstall {\n429\t            message: format!(\"Failed to create staging directory: {}\", e),\n430\t        })?;\n431\t    }\n432\t    Ok(temp_dir.join(\"forge-staged\"))\n433\t}\n434\t\n435\t/// Check if a staged update exists (for manual restart detection).\n436\t///\n437\t/// This is called at startup to detect updates that were downloaded but\n438\t/// never installed (e.g., user quit instead of auto-restarting).\n439\tpub fn has_staged_update() -> Option<PathBuf> {\n440\t    let temp_dir = std::env::temp_dir().join(\"forge-update\");\n441\t    let staging = temp_dir.join(\"forge-staged\");\n442\t    if staging.exists() {\n443\t        if let Ok(meta) = fs::metadata(&staging) {\n444\t            if meta.len() > 0 {\n445\t                return Some(staging);\n446\t            }\n447\t        }\n448\t    }\n449\t    None\n450\t}\n451\t\n452\t/// Get the final install path for the binary.\n453\t///\n454\t/// Determines the canonical install location (e.g., ~/.cargo/bin/forge).\n455\tfn get_install_path(current_exe: &Path) -> crate::Result<PathBuf> {\n456\t    // Try to determine if we're running from ~/.cargo/bin\n457\t    if let Some(home) = env::var_os(\"HOME\") {\n458\t        let cargo_bin = PathBuf::from(home).join(\".cargo\").join(\"bin\").join(\"forge\");\n459\t        if cargo_bin.exists() || current_exe == cargo_bin {\n460\t            return Ok(cargo_bin);\n461\t        }\n462\t    }\n463\t\n464\t    // Fall back to current executable location\n465\t    Ok(current_exe.to_path_buf())\n466\t}\n467\t\n468\t/// Execute a binary, replacing the current process (Unix-only).\n469\t///\n470\t/// This uses the `exec` family of syscalls to replace the current process\n471\t/// with the new binary. This function does not return on success.\n472\t#[cfg(unix)]\n473\tfn exec_binary(path: &Path, args: &[String]) -> crate::Result<()> {\n474\t    use std::ffi::CString;\n475\t    use std::os::unix::ffi::OsStrExt;\n476\t\n477\t    // Convert path to CString\n478\t    let path_cstring = CString::new(path.as_os_str().as_bytes()).map_err(|e| {\n479\t        ForgeError::UpdateInstall {\n480\t            message: format!(\"Failed to convert path to CString: {}\", e),\n481\t        }\n482\t    })?;\n483\t\n484\t    // Convert args to CString array\n485\t    let mut c_args: Vec<CString> = vec![path_cstring.clone()];\n486\t    for arg in args {\n487\t        let c_arg = CString::new(arg.as_bytes()).map_err(|e| ForgeError::UpdateInstall {\n488\t            message: format!(\"Failed to convert arg to CString: {}\", e),\n489\t        })?;\n490\t        c_args.push(c_arg);\n491\t    }\n492\t\n493\t    // Convert to raw pointers for execv\n494\t    let mut c_arg_ptrs: Vec<*const i8> = c_args.iter().map(|s| s.as_ptr()).collect();\n495\t    c_arg_ptrs.push(std::ptr::null()); // NULL-terminated array\n496\t\n497\t    // Call execv - this replaces the current process\n498\t    unsafe {\n499\t        libc::execv(path_cstring.as_ptr(), c_arg_ptrs.as_ptr());\n500\t    }\n501\t\n502\t    // If we get here, exec failed\n503\t    let errno = std::io::Error::last_os_error();\n504\t    Err(ForgeError::UpdateInstall {\n505\t        message: format!(\"execv() failed: {}\", errno),\n506\t    })\n507\t}\n508\t\n509\t/// Non-Unix platforms are not supported for self-update restart.\n510\t#[cfg(not(unix))]\n511\tfn exec_binary(_path: &Path, _args: &[String]) -> crate::Result<()> {\n512\t    Err(ForgeError::UpdateInstall {\n513\t        message: \"Self-update restart not supported on this platform\".to_string(),\n514\t    })\n515\t}\n516\t\n517\t/// Download a file with progress reporting.\n518\tasync fn download_file(\n519\t    url: &str,\n520\t    dest: &Path,\n521\t    expected_size: u64,\n522\t    progress_tx: Option<Sender<DownloadProgress>>,\n523\t) -> crate::Result<()> {\n524\t    let client = reqwest::Client::builder()\n525\t        .timeout(Duration::from_secs(DOWNLOAD_TIMEOUT_SECS))\n526\t        .user_agent(USER_AGENT)\n527\t        .build()\n528\t        .map_err(|e| ForgeError::UpdateDownload {\n529\t            message: format!(\"Failed to create HTTP client: {}\", e),\n530\t        })?;\n531\t\n532\t    let mut response = client\n533\t        .get(url)\n534\t        .send()\n535\t        .await\n536\t        .map_err(|e| ForgeError::UpdateDownload {\n537\t            message: format!(\"Failed to start download: {}\", e),\n538\t        })?;\n539\t\n540\t    if !response.status().is_success() {\n541\t        return Err(ForgeError::UpdateDownload {\n542\t            message: format!(\"Download failed with status {}\", response.status()),\n543\t        });\n544\t    }\n545\t\n546\t    // Create the destination file\n547\t    let mut file = fs::File::create(dest).map_err(|e| ForgeError::UpdateDownload {\n548\t        message: format!(\"Failed to create temp file: {}\", e),\n549\t    })?;\n550\t\n551\t    // Download in chunks with progress reporting\n552\t    let mut downloaded: u64 = 0;\n553\t\n554\t    loop {\n555\t        let chunk = response\n556\t            .chunk()\n557\t            .await\n558\t            .map_err(|e| ForgeError::UpdateDownload {\n559\t                message: format!(\"Download interrupted: {}\", e),\n560\t            })?;\n561\t\n562\t        match chunk {\n563\t            Some(chunk) => {\n564\t                file.write_all(&chunk).map_err(|e| ForgeError::UpdateDownload {\n565\t                    message: format!(\"Failed to write to temp file: {}\", e),\n566\t                })?;\n567\t\n568\t                downloaded += chunk.len() as u64;\n569\t\n570\t                // Report progress\n571\t                if let Some(ref tx) = progress_tx {\n572\t                    let percent = if expected_size > 0 {\n573\t                        ((downloaded as f64 / expected_size as f64) * 100.0) as u8\n574\t                    } else {\n575\t                        0\n576\t                    };\n577\t\n578\t                    let progress = DownloadProgress {\n579\t                        downloaded,\n580\t                        total: expected_size,\n581\t                        percent: percent.min(100),\n582\t                    };\n583\t\n584\t                    // Send progress (ignore errors if receiver is gone)\n585\t                    let _ = tx.send(progress);\n586\t                }\n587\t            }\n588\t            None => break, // End of stream\n589\t        }\n590\t    }\n591\t\n592\t    // Verify download size\n593\t    if expected_size > 0 && downloaded != expected_size {\n594\t        return Err(ForgeError::UpdateDownload {\n595\t            message: format!(\n596\t                \"Download size mismatch: expected {}, got {}\",\n597\t                expected_size, downloaded\n598\t            ),\n599\t        });\n600\t    }\n601\t\n602\t    info!(\"Download complete: {} bytes\", downloaded);\n603\t    Ok(())\n604\t}\n605\t\n606\t/// Verify the downloaded binary is a valid executable.\n607\tfn verify_binary(path: &Path) -> crate::Result<()> {\n608\t    // Check file exists and has content\n609\t    let metadata = fs::metadata(path).map_err(|e| ForgeError::UpdateVerification {\n610\t        message: format!(\"Failed to read downloaded file: {}\", e),\n611\t    })?;\n612\t\n613\t    if metadata.len() == 0 {\n614\t        return Err(ForgeError::UpdateVerification {\n615\t            message: \"Downloaded file is empty\".to_string(),\n616\t        });\n617\t    }\n618\t\n619\t    // Check ELF magic bytes (Linux executable)\n620\t    let mut file = fs::File::open(path).map_err(|e| ForgeError::UpdateVerification {\n621\t        message: format!(\"Failed to open downloaded file: {}\", e),\n622\t    })?;\n623\t\n624\t    let mut magic = [0u8; 4];\n625\t    Read::read_exact(&mut file, &mut magic).map_err(|e| ForgeError::UpdateVerification {\n626\t        message: format!(\"Failed to read file header: {}\", e),\n627\t    })?;\n628\t\n629\t    // ELF magic: 0x7f 'E' 'L' 'F'\n630\t    if magic != [0x7f, 0x45, 0x4c, 0x46] {\n631\t        return Err(ForgeError::UpdateVerification {\n632\t            message: \"Downloaded file is not a valid ELF binary\".to_string(),\n633\t        });\n634\t    }\n635\t\n636\t    info!(\"Binary verification passed (valid ELF)\");\n637\t    Ok(())\n638\t}\n639\t\n640\t/// Get the asset name for the current platform.\n641\tfn get_asset_name_for_platform() -> &'static str {\n642\t    // Currently only supporting Linux\n643\t    // Future: detect macOS, Windows, ARM architectures\n644\t    #[cfg(target_arch = \"x86_64\")]\n645\t    {\n646\t latest_parts = pad_version(&latest_parts);\n681\t\n682\t    // Compare major.minor.patch\n683\t    Ok(latest_parts > current_parts)\n684\t}\n685\t\n686\t/// Pad version components to 3 // Perform the rollback: backup.old -> current exe\n833\t    info!(\"Rolling back from {:?} to {:?}\", current_exe, backup_path);\n834\t\n835\t    // Remove current (broken) exe\n836\t    if let fs::Permissions::from_mode(0o755)) {\n849\t        error!(\"Failed to set permissions after rollback: {}\", e);\n850\t        return RollbackResult::Failed(format!(\"Failed to set permissions: {}\", Self-update functionality for FORGE binary.\n//!\n//! This module provides atomic self-update from GitHub releases:\n//! 1. Checks GitHub releases API for latest version\n//! 2. Compares with current version (semver)\n//! 3. Downloads the appropriate binary for the platform\n//! 4. Atomically swaps the running binary\n//!\n//! # Usage\n//!\n//! ```ignore\n//! use forge_core::self_update::{check_for_update, perform_update, UpdateStatus};\n//!\n//! // Check for updates\n//! let status = check_for_update(\"0.1.9\").await?;\n//! match status {\n//!     UpdateStatus::UpToDate => println!(\"Already running latest version\"),\n//!     UpdateStatus::Available { current, latest, download_url, asset_size } => {\n//!         println!(\"Update available: {} -> {}\", current, latest);\n//!         perform_update(&download_url, asset_size, |progress| {\n//!             println!(\"Downloaded {}%\", progress.percent);\n//!         }).await?;\n//!     }\n//! }\n//! ```\n\nuse std::env;\nuse std::fs;\nuse std::io::{Read, Write};\nuse std::os::unix::fs::PermissionsExt;\nuse std::path::{Path, PathBuf};\nuse std::sync::mpsc::Sender;\nuse std::time::Duration;\n\n#[allow(unused_imports)] // Used implicitly by reqwest Response::chunk()\nuse futures_util::StreamExt;\nuse serde::Deserialize;\nuse tracing::{debug, error, info, warn};\n\nuse crate::ForgeError;\n\n/// GitHub API URL for latest release\nconst GITHUB_RELEASES_API: &str = \"https://api.github.com/repos/jedarden/forge/releases/latest\";\n\n/// User agent for GitHub API requests\nconst USER_AGENT: &str = concat!(\"forge/\", env!(\"CARGO_PKG_VERSION\"));\n\n/// HTTP client timeout for API requests\nconst API_TIMEOUT_SECS: u64 = 10;\n\n/// HTTP client timeout for downloads\nconst DOWNLOAD_TIMEOUT_SECS: u64 = 300;\n\n/// Status of an update check.\n#[derive(Debug, Clone)]\npub enum UpdateStatus {\n    /// Already running the latest version\n    UpToDate,\n    /// Update available with download details\n    Available {\n        /// Current version\n        current: String,\n        /// Latest available version\n        latest: String,\n        /// URL to download the binary\n        download_url: String,\n        /// Size of the asset in bytes\n        asset_size: u64,\n    },\n}\n\n/// Progress information for download operations.\n#[derive(Debug, Clone)]\npub struct DownloadProgress {\n    /// Bytes downloaded so far\n    pub downloaded: u64,\n    /// Total bytes to download\n    pub total: u64,\n    /// Percentage complete (0-100)\n    pub percent: u8,\n}\n\n/// Result of a self-update operation.\n#[derive(Debug, Clone)]\npub enum UpdateResult {\n    /// Update completed successfully\n    Success {\n        /// Previous version\n        old_version: String,\n        /// New version\n        new_version: String,\n    },\n    /// Update failed with error message\n    Failed(String),\n    /// Already up to date\n    AlreadyUpToDate,\n}\n\n/// GitHub release asset information.\n#[derive(Debug, Deserialize)]\nstruct GitHubAsset {\n    name: String,\n    #[serde(rename = \"browser_download_url\")]\n    download_url: String,\n    size: u64,\n    state: String,\n}\n\n/// GitHub release information from API.\n#[derive(Debug, Deserialize)]\nstruct GitHubRelease {\n    #[serde(rename = \"tag_name\")]\n    tag_name: String,\n    assets: Vec<GitHubAsset>,\n}\n\n/// Check for available updates from GitHub releases.\n///\n/// # Arguments\n///\n/// * `current_version` - Current version string (e.g., \"0.1.9\")\n///\n/// # Returns\n///\n/// - `UpdateStatus::UpToDate` if already on latest version\n/// - `UpdateStatus::Available` with download details if update available\n/// - `ForgeError` on network or parsing errors\npub async fn check_for_update(current_version: &str) -> crate::Result<UpdateStatus> {\n    info!(\"Checking for updates (current: {})\", current_version);\n\n    let client = reqwest::Client::builder()\n        .timeout(Duration::from_secs(API_TIMEOUT_SECS))\n        .user_agent(USER_AGENT)\n        .build()\n        .map_err(|e| ForgeError::UpdateCheck {\n            message: format!(\"Failed to create HTTP client: {}\", e),\n        })?;\n\n    let response = client\n        .get(GITHUB_RELEASES_API)\n        .send()\n        .await\n        .map_err(|e| ForgeError::UpdateCheck {\n            message: format!(\"Failed to fetch releases: {}\", e),\n        })?;\n\n    if !response.status().is_success() {\n        return Err(ForgeError::UpdateCheck {\n            message: format!(\"GitHub API returned status {}\", response.status()),\n        });\n    }\n\n    let release: GitHubRelease = response\n        .json()\n        .await\n        .map_err(|e| ForgeError::UpdateCheck {\n            message: format!(\"Failed to parse release response: {}\", e),\n        })?;\n\n    // Parse version from tag (e.g., \"v0.1.9\" -> \"0.1.9\")\n    let latest_version = release.tag_name.strip_prefix('v').unwrap_or(&release.tag_name);\n\n    info!(\"Latest version: {}\", latest_version);\n\n    // Compare versions using semver\n    if !is_newer_version(current_version, latest_version)? {\n        info!(\"Already running latest version\");\n        return Ok(UpdateStatus::UpToDate);\n    }\n\n    // Find the appropriate asset for this platform\n    let asset_name = get_asset_name_for_platform();\n    let asset = release\n        .assets\n        .iter()\n        .find(|a| a.name == asset_name && a.state == \"uploaded\")\n        .ok_or_else(|| ForgeError::UpdateAssetNotFound {\n            platform: asset_name.to_string(),\n        })?;\n\n    info!(\n        \"Update available: {} -> {} ({} bytes)\",\n        current_version, latest_version, asset.size\n    );\n\n    Ok(UpdateStatus::Available {\n        current: current_version.to_string(),\n        latest: latest_version.to_string(),\n        download_url: asset.download_url.clone(),\n        asset_size: asset.size,\n    })\n}\n\n/// Perform the self-update: download and atomic swap.\n///\n/// # Arguments\n///\n/// * `download_url` - URL to download the binary from\n/// * `expected_size` - Expected size of the download in bytes\n/// * `progress_tx` - Optional channel to send progress updates\n///\n/// # Returns\n///\n/// - `UpdateResult::Success` on successful update\n/// - `UpdateResult::Failed` with error message on failure\npub async fn perform_update(\n    download_url: &str,\n    expected_size: u64,\n    progress_tx: Option<Sender<DownloadProgress>>,\n) -> crate::Result<UpdateResult> {\n    info!(\"Starting update download from {}\", download_url);\n\n    // Get current executable path\n    let current_exe = env::current_exe().map_err(|e| ForgeError::UpdateInstall {\n        message: format!(\"Failed to get current executable path: {}\", e),\n    })?;\n\n    // Download to a staging file\n    let staging_file = get_staging_path(&current_exe)?;\n\n    info!(\"Downloading to staging file: {:?}\", staging_file);\n\n    // Download the new binary\n    download_file(download_url, &staging_file, expected_size, progress_tx).await?;\n\n    // Verify the downloaded file is a valid executable\n    verify_binary(&staging_file)?;\n\n    info!(\"Update download complete! Binary staged at {:?}\", staging_file);\n\n    Ok(UpdateResult::Success {\n        old_version: env!(\"CARGO_PKG_VERSION\").to_string(),\n        new_version: \"latest\".to_string(), // We don't have this info here anymore\n    })\n}\n\n/// Restart the process using the newly downloaded binary.\n///\n/// This function performs the following steps:\n/// 1. Gracefully shutdown current process (caller's responsibility)\n/// 2. Exec the new binary from staging location\n/// 3. New process will rename itself to the final location\n///\n/// This function DOES NOT RETURN on success - it replaces the current process.\n/// On error, it returns a ForgeError.\npub fn restart_with_new_binary() -> crate::Result<()> {\n    info!(\"Initiating restart with new binary\");\n\n    // Get current executable path\n    let current_exe = env::current_exe().map_err(|e| ForgeError::UpdateInstall {\n        message: format!(\"Failed to get current executable path: {}\", e),\n    })?;\n\n    // Get staging path\n    let staging_file = get_staging_path(&current_exe)?;\n\n    // Verify staging file exists\n    if !staging_file.exists() {\n        return Err(ForgeError::UpdateInstall {\n            message: format!(\"Staging file not found at {:?}\", staging_file),\n        });\n    }\n\n    info!(\"Staging file found at {:?}\", staging_file);\n\n    // Verify the staging file is executable\n    verify_binary(&staging_file)?;\n\n    // Get the final install path (e.g., ~/.cargo/bin/forge)\n    let install_path = get_install_path(&current_exe)?;\n\n    info!(\n        \"Will exec staging binary and install to {:?}\",\n        install_path\n    );\n\n    // Set env vars directly in the process before execv() — exec inherits\n    // the current environment. We must set these here (not on a Command\n    // object) because exec_binary() uses raw execv(), not std::process::Command.\n    // SAFETY: This is safe here because we are about to exec() — no other\n    // threads can observe the inconsistent env state. The exec syscall\n    // replaces the entire process image.\n    unsafe {\n        env::set_var(\"FORGE_INSTALL_PATH\", &install_path);\n        env::set_var(\"FORGE_STAGING_PATH\", &staging_file);\n        env::set_var(\"FORGE_AUTO_RESTART\", \"1\");\n    }\n\n    // Preserve current args\n    let args: Vec<String> = env::args().skip(1).collect();\n\n    info!(\n        \"Execing new binary: {:?} with args: {:?}\",\n        staging_file, args\n    );\n\n    // Replace current process with new binary using exec\n    // On Unix, use exec syscall to replace the process\n    exec_binary(&staging_file, &args)?;\n\n    // This line should never be reached if exec succeeds\n    unreachable!(\"exec() returned, which should never happen\");\n}\n\n/// Check if a staged update needs to be installed.\n///\n/// This handles two scenarios:\n/// 1. Auto-restart: env vars FORGE_AUTO_RESTART, FORGE_INSTALL_PATH, FORGE_STAGING_PATH\n///    are set by the old process before execv()\n/// 2. Manual restart: a stale staging file exists from a previous update that was\n///    downloaded but the user quit instead of auto-restarting\n///\n/// Returns the install path if an update was installed, None otherwise.\npub fn check_and_perform_self_install() -> crate::Result<Option<PathBuf>> {\n    // Determine staging and install paths\n    let (staging_path, install_path) = if env::var(\"FORGE_AUTO_RESTART\").is_ok() {\n        // Auto-restart path: env vars from old process\n        info!(\"Detected auto-restart environment - performing self-install\");\n\n        let install_path_str = env::var(\"FORGE_INSTALL_PATH\").map_err(|_| {\n            ForgeError::UpdateInstall {\n                message: \"FORGE_INSTALL_PATH not set\".to_string(),\n            }\n        })?;\n        let staging_path_str = env::var(\"FORGE_STAGING_PATH\").map_err(|_| {\n            ForgeError::UpdateInstall {\n                message: \"FORGE_STAGING_PATH not set\".to_string(),\n            }\n        })?;\n        (PathBuf::from(staging_path_str), PathBuf::from(install_path_str))\n    } else if let Some(staged) = has_staged_update() {\n        // Manual restart path: stale staging file detected\n        info!(\"Detected staged update from previous session - installing\");\n\n        let current_exe = env::current_exe().map_err(|e| ForgeError::UpdateInstall {\n            message: format!(\"Failed to get current executable path: {}\", e),\n        })?;\n        let install = get_install_path(&current_exe)?;\n        (staged, install)\n    } else {\n        return Ok(None);\n    };\n\n    // Verify staging file still exists and is valid\n    if !staging_path.exists() {\n        warn!(\"Staging file disappeared: {:?}\", staging_path);\n        return Ok(None);\n    }\n\n    if let Err(e) = verify_binary(&staging_path) {\n        warn!(\"Staged binary failed verification, removing: {}\", e);\n        let _ = fs::remove_file(&staging_path);\n        return Ok(None);\n    }\n\n    info!(\n        \"Installing from {:?} to {:?}\",\n        staging_path, install_path\n    );\n\n    // Create backup of old binary\n    let backup_path = install_path.with_extension(\"old\");\n    if install_path.exists() {\n        info!(\"Backing up old binary to {:?}\", backup_path);\n        if backup_path.exists() {\n            fs::remove_file(&backup_path).map_err(|e| ForgeError::UpdateInstall {\n                message: format!(\"Failed to remove old backup: {}\", e),\n            })?;\n        }\n        fs::rename(&install_path, &backup_path).map_err(|e| ForgeError::UpdateInstall {\n            message: format!(\"Failed to backup old binary: {}\", e),\n        })?;\n    }\n\n    // Move staging binary to install location.\n    // rename() works on Linux even for running binaries (atomic directory op).\n    // If cross-filesystem, fall back to copy+delete.\n    let move_result = fs::rename(&staging_path, &install_path);\n    if let Err(e) = move_result {\n        // Cross-filesystem fallback: copy then delete\n        info!(\"rename() failed ({}), falling back to copy\", e);\n        fs::copy(&staging_path, &install_path).map_err(|e2| {\n            // Try to restore backup on failure\n            if backup_path.exists() {\n                let _ = fs::rename(&backup_path, &install_path);\n            }\n            ForgeError::UpdateInstall {\n                message: format!(\"Failed to install new binary: {}\", e2),\n            }\n        })?;\n        let _ = fs::remove_file(&staging_path);\n    }\n\n    // Set executable permissions\n    fs::set_permissions(&install_path, fs::Permissions::from_mode(0o755)).map_err(|e| {\n        ForgeError::UpdateInstall {\n            message: format!(\"Failed to set executable permissions: {}\", e),\n        }\n    })?;\n\n    // Clean up environment variables (no-op if not set)\n    // SAFETY: These environment variables are only used during the update process\n    // and are safe to remove as we're done with them.\n    unsafe {\n        env::remove_var(\"FORGE_AUTO_RESTART\");\n        env::remove_var(\"FORGE_INSTALL_PATH\");\n        env::remove_var(\"FORGE_STAGING_PATH\");\n    }\n\n    // Save the new version to ~/.forge/version\n    let current_version = env!(\"CARGO_PKG_VERSION\");\n    if let Err(e) = save_current_version(current_version) {\n        warn!(\"Failed to save version file: {}\", e);\n    }\n\n    info!(\"Self-install complete! Running from {:?}\", install_path);\n\n    Ok(Some(install_path))\n}\n\n/// Get the staging path for the downloaded binary.\n///\n/// Uses a stable path (not PID-dependent) so the staged update survives\n/// manual restarts. The staging file is placed in a forge-specific temp dir.\nfn get_staging_path(_current_exe: &Path) -> crate::Result<PathBuf> {\n    let temp_dir = std::env::temp_dir().join(\"forge-update\");\n    if !temp_dir.exists() {\n        fs::create_dir_all(&temp_dir).map_err(|e| ForgeError::UpdateInstall {\n            message: format!(\"Failed to create staging directory: {}\", e),\n        })?;\n    }\n    Ok(temp_dir.join(\"forge-staged\"))\n}\n\n/// Check if a staged update exists (for manual restart detection).\n///\n/// This is called at startup to detect updates that were downloaded but\n/// never installed (e.g., user quit instead of auto-restarting).\npub fn has_staged_update() -> Option<PathBuf> {\n    let temp_dir = std::env::temp_dir().join(\"forge-update\");\n    let staging = temp_dir.join(\"forge-staged\");\n    if staging.exists() {\n        if let Ok(meta) = fs::metadata(&staging) {\n            if meta.len() > 0 {\n                return Some(staging);\n            }\n        }\n    }\n    None\n}\n\n/// Get the final install path for the binary.\n///\n/// Determines the canonical install location (e.g., ~/.cargo/bin/forge).\nfn get_install_path(current_exe: &Path) -> crate::Result<PathBuf> {\n    // Try to determine if we're running from ~/.cargo/bin\n    if let Some(home) = env::var_os(\"HOME\") {\n        let cargo_bin = PathBuf::from(home).join(\".cargo\").join(\"bin\").join(\"forge\");\n        if cargo_bin.exists() || current_exe == cargo_bin {\n            return Ok(cargo_bin);\n        }\n    }\n\n    // Fall back to current executable location\n    Ok(current_exe.to_path_buf())\n}\n\n/// Execute a binary, replacing the current process (Unix-only).\n///\n/// This uses the `exec` family of syscalls to replace the current process\n/// with the new binary. This function does not return on success.\n#[cfg(unix)]\nfn exec_binary(path: &Path, args: &[String]) -> crate::Result<()> {\n    use std::ffi::CString;\n    use std::os::unix::ffi::OsStrExt;\n\n    // Convert path to CString\n    let path_cstring = CString::new(path.as_os_str().as_bytes()).map_err(|e| {\n        ForgeError::UpdateInstall {\n            message: format!(\"Failed to convert path to CString: {}\", e),\n        }\n    })?;\n\n    // Convert args to CString array\n    let mut c_args: Vec<CString> = vec![path_cstring.clone()];\n    for arg in args {\n        let c_arg = CString::new(arg.as_bytes()).map_err(|e| ForgeError::UpdateInstall {\n            message: format!(\"Failed to convert arg to CString: {}\", e),\n        })?;\n        c_args.push(c_arg);\n    }\n\n    // Convert to raw pointers for execv\n    let mut c_arg_ptrs: Vec<*const i8> = c_args.iter().map(|s| s.as_ptr()).collect();\n    c_arg_ptrs.push(std::ptr::null()); // NULL-terminated array\n\n    // Call execv - this replaces the current process\n    unsafe {\n        libc::execv(path_cstring.as_ptr(), c_arg_ptrs.as_ptr());\n    }\n\n    // If we get here, exec failed\n    let errno = std::io::Error::last_os_error();\n    Err(ForgeError::UpdateInstall {\n        message: format!(\"execv() failed: {}\", errno),\n    })\n}\n\n/// Non-Unix platforms are not supported for self-update restart.\n#[cfg(not(unix))]\nfn exec_binary(_path: &Path, _args: &[String]) -> crate::Result<()> {\n    Err(ForgeError::UpdateInstall {\n        message: \"Self-update restart not supported on this platform\".to_string(),\n    })\n}\n\n/// Download a file with progress reporting.\nasync fn download_file(\n    url: &str,\n    dest: &Path,\n    expected_size: u64,\n    progress_tx: Option<Sender<DownloadProgress>>,\n) -> crate::Result<()> {\n    let client = reqwest::Client::builder()\n        .timeout(Duration::from_secs(DOWNLOAD_TIMEOUT_SECS))\n        .user_agent(USER_AGENT)\n        .build()\n        .map_err(|e| ForgeError::UpdateDownload {\n            message: format!(\"Failed to create HTTP client: {}\", e),\n        })?;\n\n    let mut response = client\n        .get(url)\n        .send()\n        .await\n        .map_err(|e| ForgeError::UpdateDownload {\n            message: format!(\"Failed to start download: {}\", e),\n        })?;\n\n    if !response.status().is_success() {\n        return Err(ForgeError::UpdateDownload {\n            message: format!(\"Download failed with status {}\", response.status()),\n        });\n    }\n\n    // Create the destination file\n    let mut file = fs::File::create(dest).map_err(|e| ForgeError::UpdateDownload {\n        message: format!(\"Failed to create temp file: {}\", e),\n    })?;\n\n    // Download in chunks with progress reporting\n    let mut downloaded: u64 = 0;\n\n    loop {\n        let chunk = response\n            .chunk()\n            .await\n            .map_err(|e| ForgeError::UpdateDownload {\n                message: format!(\"Download interrupted: {}\", e),\n            })?;\n\n        match chunk {\n            Some(chunk) => {\n                file.write_all(&chunk).map_err(|e| ForgeError::UpdateDownload {\n                    message: format!(\"Failed to write to temp file: {}\", e),\n                })?;\n\n                downloaded += chunk.len() as u64;\n\n                // Report progress\n                if let Some(ref tx) = progress_tx {\n                    let percent = if expected_size > 0 {\n                        ((downloaded as f64 / expected_size as f64) * 100.0) as u8\n                    } else {\n                        0\n                    };\n\n                    let progress = DownloadProgress {\n                        downloaded,\n                        total: expected_size,\n                        percent: percent.min(100),\n                    };\n\n                    // Send progress (ignore errors if receiver is gone)\n                    let _ = tx.send(progress);\n                }\n            }\n            None => break, // End of stream\n        }\n    }\n\n    // Verify download size\n    if expected_size > 0 && downloaded != expected_size {\n        return Err(ForgeError::UpdateDownload {\n            message: format!(\n                \"Download size mismatch: expected {}, got {}\",\n                expected_size, downloaded\n            ),\n        });\n    }\n\n    info!(\"Download complete: {} bytes\", downloaded);\n    Ok(())\n}\n\n/// Verify the downloaded binary is a valid executable.\nfn verify_binary(path: &Path) -> crate::Result<()> {\n    // Check file exists and has content\n    let metadata = fs::metadata(path).map_err(|e| ForgeError::UpdateVerification {\n        message: format!(\"Failed to read downloaded file: {}\", e),\n    })?;\n\n    if metadata.len() == 0 {\n        return Err(ForgeError::UpdateVerification {\n            message: \"Downloaded file is empty\".to_string(),\n        });\n    }\n\n    // Check ELF magic bytes (Linux executable)\n    let mut file = fs::File::open(path).map_err(|e| ForgeError::UpdateVerification {\n        message: format!(\"Failed to open downloaded file: {}\", e),\n    })?;\n\n    let mut magic = [0u8; 4];\n    Read::read_exact(&mut file, &mut magic).map_err(|e| ForgeError::UpdateVerification {\n        message: format!(\"Failed to read file header: {}\", e),\n    })?;\n\n    // ELF magic: 0x7f 'E' 'L' 'F'\n    if magic != [0x7f, 0x45, // Future: detect macOS, Windows, ARM architectures\n    #[cfg(target_arch = \"x86_64\")]\n    {\n        \"forge\"\n    }\n    #[cfg(target_arch = \"aarch64\")]\n    {\n        \"forge-linux-aarch64\"\n    }\n    #[cfg(not(any(target_arch = \"x86_64\", target_arch = \"aarch64\")))]\n    {\n        \"forge\"\n    }\n}\n\n/// Compare two version strings to determine if the second is newer.\n///\n/// Uses semantic versioning comparison (major.minor.patch).\nfn is_newer_version(current: &str, latest: &str) -> crate::Result<bool> {\n    let current_parts: Vec<u32> = current\n        .split('.')\n        .filter_map(|s| s.parse().ok())\n        .collect();\n\n    let latest_parts: Vec<u32> = latest\n        .split('.')\n        .filter_map(|s| s.parse().ok())\n        .collect();\n\n    if current_parts.is_empty() || latest_parts.is_empty() {\n        return Err(ForgeError::UpdateCheck {\n            message: format!(\"Invalid version format: {} or {}\", current, latest),\n        });\n    }\n\n    // Pad to 3 components (major.minor.patch)\n    let current_parts = pad_version(&current_parts);\n    let latest_parts = pad_version(&latest_parts);\n\n    // Compare major.minor.patch\n    Ok(latest_parts > current_parts)\n}\n\n/// Pad version components to 3 elements.\nfn pad_version(parts: &[u32]) -> [u32; 3] {\n    let mut result = [0u32; 3];\n    for (i, &part) in parts.iter().enumerate().take(3) {\n        result[i] = part;\n    }\n    result\n}\n\n/// Get the path to the version tracking file (~/.forge/version).\nfn get_version_file_path() directory exists\n    if let Some(parent) = version_file.parent() {\n        fs::create_dir_all(parent).map_err(|e| ForgeError::UpdateInstall {\n            message: format!(\"Failed to create .forge will be deleted on successful startup.\npub fn mark_startup_in_progress() -> crate::Result<()> {\n    let marker_file = get_startup_marker_path();\n\n    // Ensure parent directory exists\n    if let /// Successfully rolled back from backup\n    RolledBack {\n        /// Version that was rolled back from\n        failed_version: String,\n        /// Version rolled back to (if known)\n        restored_version: Option<String>,\n    },\n    /// No rollback needed (no crash detected)\n    NotNeeded,\n    /// Rollback failed (backup not found or other error)\n    Failed(String),\n}\n\n/// Attempt to rollback to the .old backup if startup crashed.\n///\n/// This should be called at the very beginning of main() before any other initialization.\n///\n/// Returns:\n/// - `RollbackResult::RolledBack` if rollback was performed\n/// - `RollbackResult::NotNeeded` if no crash was detected\n/// - `RollbackResult::Failed` if rollback was needed but failed\npub fn check_and_rollback() -> RollbackResult {\n    // Check if previous startup crashed\n    if !did_previous_startup_crash() {\n        return RollbackResult::NotNeeded;\n    }\n\n    warn!(\"Detected crash on previous startup, attempting rollback...\");\n\n    // Get current executable path\n    let current_exe = match env::current_exe() {\n        Ok(path) => path,\n        Err(e) => {\n            error!(\"Failed to get current executable path: {}\", e);\n            return RollbackResult::Failed(format!(\"Failed to get executable path: {}\", e));\n        }\n    };\n\n    let backup_path = current_exe.with_extension(\"old\");\n\n    // Check if backup exists\n    if !backup_path.exists() {\n        error!(\"Backup file not found: {:?}\", backup_path);\n        // Clean up the marker file since we can't rollback\n        let _ = fs::remove_file(get_startup_marker_path());\n        return RollbackResult::Failed(\"Backup file not found\".to_string());\n    }\n\n    // Read the failed version (current version before rollback)\n    let failed_version = env!(\"CARGO_PKG_VERSION\").to_string();\n\n    // Perform the rollback: backup.old -> current exe\n    info!(\"Rolling back from {:?} to {:?}\", current_exe, backup_path);\n\n    // Remove current (broken) exe\n    if let Err(e) = fs::remove_file(&current_exe) {\n        error!(\"Failed to remove broken binary: {}\", e);\n        return RollbackResult::Failed(format!(\"Failed to remove broken binary: {}\", e));\n    }\n\n    // Restore from backup\n    if let Err(e) = fs::copy(&backup_path, &current_exe) {\n        error!(\"Failed to restore from backup: {}\", e);\n        return RollbackResult::Failed(format!(\"Failed to restore from backup: {}\", e));\n    }\n\n    // Set executable permissions\n    if let Err(e) = fs::set_permissions(&current_exe, fs::Permissions::from_mode(0o755)) {\n        error!(\"Failed to set permissions after rollback: {}\", e);\n        return RollbackResult::Failed(format!(\"Failed to set permissions: {}\", e));\n    }\n\n    // Clean up marker file\n    let _ = fs::remove_file(get_startup_marker_path());\n\n    // Get the restored version from the version file (if it exists)\n    let restored_version = read_last_version();\n\n    info!(\"Rollback successful! Restored from backup.\");\n\n    RollbackResult::RolledBack {\n        failed_version,\n        restored_version,\n    }\n}\n\n#[cfg(test)]\nmod tests {\n    use super::*;\n    use serial_test::serial;\n\n    #[test]\n    fn test_version_comparison() {\n        // Basic comparisons\n        assert!(is_newer_version(\"0.1.0\", \"0.1.1\").unwrap());\n The fix was implemented in commits:\n- `aec5f73` - Fixed env var propagation and staging path issues\n- `7ffe04e` - Fixed missing should_quit to trigger restart\n\n## How the fix works\n\nThe self-update flow now correctly avoids overwriting the running binary:\n\n1. **Download to staging**: `perform_update()` downloads the new binary to `/tmp/forge-update/forge-staged` (not the final location)\n2. **Trigger restart**: After successful download, `should_quit = true` is set, causing the main loop to exit\n3. **Exec staging binary**: `restart_with_new_binary()` sets env vars (FORGE_AUTO_RESTART, FORGE_INSTALL_PATH, FORGE_STAGING_PATH) and execs the staging binary\n4. **Self-install on startup**: The new binary detects the restart env vars in `check_and_perform_self_install()` and installs itself to `~/.cargo/bin/forge`\n\n## Key fixes from aec5f73\n\n1. **Env vars set directly**: Used `std::env::set_var()` instead of setting on a Command object (which was ignored by execv())\n2. **Stable staging path**: Changed from PID-based filename to stable `/tmp/forge-update/forge-staged` so manual restarts work\n3. **Manual restart detection**: Added fallback to detect stale staging files for users who quit instead of auto-restarting\n\n## Retrospective\n\n- **What worked:** The atomic staging + exec approach completely avoids the ETXTBSY error. The running binary is never overwritten—instead, we exec a new binary that installs itself on startup.\n- **What didn't:** The original cargo build + cp approach was fundamentally flawed because it tried to overwrite a running executable.
